It is called the **\"Action-Based Language Switcher.\"**\n\nHere is why it works this way:\n\n### 1. The \"Switch To\" Logic (What we are using)\nRight now, the button shows the language you *will switch to*, not the language you are currently in. \n- When the app is in **Urdu**, the button says **\"English (EN)\"**.\n- **Why?** Imagine a farmer opens the app, and the entire app is in Urdu. But the farmer only reads English. They will immediately look for the word **\"English\"** on the screen to click on it.
